# Compliance Audit: Envoy Access Logging Configuration Coverage

## Your Task

Also find the corresponding `.proto` definitions in `envoyproxy/data-plane-api` under `envoy/extensions/access_loggers/`. For each implementation, report whether it supports structured (JSON) logging or only unstructured text logging.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the compliance domain.

{
  "message": "The audit is complete. `/workspace/answer.json` (31,820 bytes, valid JSON) contains the full audit of Envoy's access logging infrastructure across both repositories.\n\n**Key findings:**\n\n- **File, Stdout, Stderr loggers** support both structured JSON and unstructured text, controlled by the `log_format` (`SubstitutionFormatString`) field. The file logger also has deprecated `json_format`/`typed_json_format` Struct fields.\n\n- **HTTP gRPC and TCP gRPC ALS loggers** support neither JSON nor text \u2014 they emit binary Protocol Buffers (`HTTPAccessLogEntry` / `TCPAccessLogEntry`) over a bidirectional gRPC stream to an ALS server.\n\n- **OpenTelemetry logger** supports neither JSON nor text \u2014 it emits OTLP binary protobuf (`ExportLogsServiceRequest` with `LogRecord` containing `KeyValueList` body/attributes) over OTLP/gRPC or OTLP/HTTP. The body/attributes fields use Envoy format specifiers as template strings, but the wire encoding is always protobuf.\n\n- **Fluentd logger** supports structured output only (no plain text) \u2014 it always produces MessagePack binary using the Fluentd Forward Protocol, internally converting a JSON-formatted `record` Struct to MessagePack via `Json::Factory::jsonToMsgpack()`.\n\n- **Wasm logger** is entirely plugin-dependent \u2014 Envoy performs no formatting; the WASM plugin's `on_log()` ABI function has full control.\n\n- **CEL filter** and all built-in filters (`StatusCodeFilter`, `DurationFilter`, etc.) are predicates only \u2014 they suppress or allow log emission but produce no output themselves.\n\n- **Stats logger**, **Dynamic Modules logger**, and **ProcessRateLimit filter** have proto definitions in data-plane-api but no C++ implementation in the v1.31.2 source tree."
